3/9/24, 6:24 PM - +91 90511 97772: Well, I don't know if you'd get me but how certain are you that given there are IQ tests in the training data of Claude 3/GPT 4, it boosts the IQ points by significant measure where among n test sessions, the median score is far off from the real score? While it's true that one can prepare for IQ tests to some extent, the assertion that "you can prepare for IQ tests and get a few points boosted" oversimplifies the complexity of intelligence testing. IQ tests measure a range of cognitive abilities, including problem-solving, pattern recognition, and logical reasoning, which are not solely dependent on preparation but also on inherent cognitive abilities. But let's just say I'm wrong and you can boost your points in an IQ test. Okay, let's take the fact that training data leads to chain of thought reasoning, the in that case, lets generalize the questions in iq tests. they are logical questions? agree right? take the fact that a human sees so many logical questions before the average human takes an iq test, then would that not lead to chain of thought reasoning in human neural systems leading to the same fallacy that you say is occuring in AI models? 

The comparison of human brain power and AI model power intake is inherently flawed because they both operate on different mechanisms and silicion life and carbon based life can operate on different levels of power intake and still have the same intelligence
